</p>
<ol><li>organization, arrangement

<li>organization
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организация.html>организа́ция</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:объединённый.html>Объединённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нация.html>на́ций</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Organizácija Obʺjedinjónnyx Nácij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">United Nations Organization</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>setup, structure
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:организация.html>организа́ция</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сеть.html>сети</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>organizácija</b> seti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">networking</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***организм.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:организм.html>органи́зм</a> (1378)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">organisme</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организм.html>органи́зм</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">organízm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организм.html>органи́зма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организм.html>органи́змы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организм.html>органи́змов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>system of organs making up the body of a living thing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">перееда́ть <a href = vnd.unilang:вредный.html>вре́дно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́шего</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:организм.html>органи́зма</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Perejedátʹ vrédno dlja náševo <b>organízma</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Overeating is bad for our <b>bodies</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>organism (living thing, usually a small and simplistic one)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a complex structure or mechanism</li></ol>

<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ōrdinārius</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оренбургский.html>оренбу́ргский</a> (27871)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">оренбу́рг</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Orenbúrg</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***орех.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a> (4636)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orěxъ</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq">arrë</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">walnut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἄρυα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">árua</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">walnut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">riẽksts</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">òrah</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oréx</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́ха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́хов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nut <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">tree; seed</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бразильский.html>брази́льский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">brazílʹskij <b>oréx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Brazil nut (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Bertholletia_excelsa" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Bertholletia excelsa"><i>Bertholletia excelsa</i></a></span>)</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">Brazilian <b>nut</b></span>”)</div></dd>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oréx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ореховый.html>оре́ховый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oréxovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ореховый.html>оре́ховая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорлупа.html>скорлупа́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oréxovaja</b> skorlupá</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>nut</b>shell</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> walnut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ореховый.html>оре́ховый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлеб.html>хлеб</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oréxovyj</b> xleb</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>walnut</b> bread</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>walnut, nut-brown <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">color</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oréx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орешек.html>оре́шек</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oréšek</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орешек.html>оре́шка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орешек.html>оре́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орешек.html>оре́шков</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оригинал.html>оригина́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">originál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оригинал.html>оригина́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оригинал.html>оригина́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оригинал.html>оригина́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>original (object from which all later copies and variations are derived)</li>
<li>eccentric</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ри<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ги<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>на́л</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:неординарный.html>неордина́рный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a> (<span title="в винительном падеже"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</span> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:оригинал.html>оригина́ла</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:оригинал.html>оригина́лов</a></i>).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-оригинал-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оригинальный.html>оригина́льный</a> (4873)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ри<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ги<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>на́ль<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

***ориентация.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ориентация.html>ориента́ция</a> (9940)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ориентация.html>ориента́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">orijentácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ориентация.html>ориента́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ориентация.html>ориента́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ориентация.html>ориента́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>orientation</li>
<li>understanding</li>
<li>direction of attention
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ориентация.html>ориента́ция</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> что́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>orijentácija</b> na štó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">focus on something</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
